# Obtuse Perfect Polyiamond Regex Search Results

**Files searched:** obtuse_12.txt, obtuse_18.txt, obtuse_24.txt, obtuse_30.txt, obtuse_36.txt, obtuse_42.txt, obtuse_48.txt

**Patterns tested:** 20 (subsets of 3 or 4 pairs from {AB, AF, CB, CD, ED, EF}, always including AB)

**Patterns with matches:** 4

## Summary

| Pattern | Matches | Min trans. | Max trans. | Filter file |
|---------|---------|------------|------------|-------------|
| `^(AB|AF|CB|ED)*$` | 211 | 4 | 15 | `filter_AB_AF_CB_ED.txt` |
| `^(AB|AF|CD|EF)*$` | 1720 | 4 | 17 | `filter_AB_AF_CD_EF.txt` |
| `^(AB|CB|CD|EF)*$` | 176 | 5 | 16 | `filter_AB_CB_CD_EF.txt` |
| `^(AB|CD|ED|EF)*$` | 250 | 5 | 16 | `filter_AB_CD_ED_EF.txt` |
